Our friends at [Johto Times](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Johto_Times "Johto Times") are currently running a poll to determine **[the ultimate fan-favorite Pokémon!](https://johto.substack.com/p/johto-times-favourite-pokemon-poll-2025)**

Please remember to follow the [unreleased materials policy](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Bulbapedia:Unreleased_materials_policy "Bulbapedia:Unreleased materials policy"), [manual of style](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Bulbapedia:Manual_of_style "Bulbapedia:Manual of style"), and [code of conduct](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Bulbapedia:Code_of_conduct "Bulbapedia:Code of conduct") at all times.

Check the [Bulbagarden home page](https://bulbagarden.net/) for up-to-date Pokémon news, and discuss it on the [forums](https://bulbagarden.net/forums/) or in the [Bulbagarden Discord server](https://discord.gg/bulbagarden).

# Walkthrough:Pokémon FireRed and LeafGreen/Part 10

From Bulbapedia, the community-driven Pokémon encyclopedia.

< [Walkthrough:Pokémon FireRed and LeafGreen](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Walkthrough:Pok%C3%A9mon_FireRed_and_LeafGreen "Walkthrough:Pokémon FireRed and LeafGreen")

[Jump to navigation](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Walkthrough:Pok%C3%A9mon_FireRed_and_LeafGreen/Part_10#column-one) [Jump to search](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Walkthrough:Pok%C3%A9mon_FireRed_and_LeafGreen/Part_10#searchInput)

_This is the Bulbapedia walkthrough for [Pokémon FireRed and LeafGreen](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_FireRed_and_LeafGreen_Versions "Pokémon FireRed and LeafGreen Versions")._

_These pages follow the remade [Game Boy Advance](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Game_Boy_Advance "Game Boy Advance") iteration, **not** [Pokémon Red and Blue](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Red_and_Blue_Versions "Pokémon Red and Blue Versions"). The guide for those games can be found **[here](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Walkthrough:Pok%C3%A9mon_Red_and_Blue "Walkthrough:Pokémon Red and Blue")**._

* * *

## Route 12

[![](https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/b/be/Kanto_Route_12_FRLG.png/75px-Kanto_Route_12_FRLG.png)](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/File:Kanto_Route_12_FRLG.png) Route 12

[Route 12](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto_Route_12 "Kanto Route 12") connects [Lavender Town](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Lavender_Town "Lavender Town"), [Route 11](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto_Route_11 "Kanto Route 11"), and [Route 13](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto_Route_13 "Kanto Route 13"). Beyond the northern gate, the area is also known as Silence Bridge. It is a favorite spot for Fishermen.

### Roadblock

Halfway through the route, a second [Snorlax](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Snorlax_(Pok%C3%A9mon) "Snorlax (Pokémon)") has fallen asleep in another inconvenient place. Use the [Poké Flute](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Pok%C3%A9_Flute "Poké Flute") like before to wake the Pokémon, and it attacks in a grumpy rage!

### Fishing Guru 3

The house to the south of the intersection with [Route 11](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto_Route_11 "Kanto Route 11") is home to the [Fishing Guru](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Fishing_Brothers "Fishing Brothers")'s younger brother. Speak to him to receive the [Super Rod](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Super_Rod "Super Rod"). This high-end fishing rod is the best model available and can reel in some of the strongest sea creatures, like [Seaking](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Seaking_(Pok%C3%A9mon) "Seaking (Pokémon)") and [Dratini](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Dratini_(Pok%C3%A9mon) "Dratini (Pokémon)").

## Route 13

[![](https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/d/d4/Kanto_Route_13_FRLG.png/300px-Kanto_Route_13_FRLG.png)](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/File:Kanto_Route_13_FRLG.png) Route 13

[Route 13](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto_Route_13 "Kanto Route 13") is a difficult, narrow path that leads westward to [Route 14](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto_Route_14 "Kanto Route 14"). Many Trainers can be found among the maze of fences.

## Route 14

[![](https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/0/08/Kanto_Route_14_FRLG.png/100px-Kanto_Route_14_FRLG.png)](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/File:Kanto_Route_14_FRLG.png) Route 14

[Route 14](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto_Route_14 "Kanto Route 14") is a pleasant coastal road where the salty breeze blows in from the sea. The path runs south to [Route 15](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto_Route_15 "Kanto Route 15").

## Route 15

[![](https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/a/ab/Kanto_Route_15_FRLG.png/300px-Kanto_Route_15_FRLG.png)](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/File:Kanto_Route_15_FRLG.png) Route 15

[Route 15](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto_Route_15 "Kanto Route 15") leads west from [Route 14](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto_Route_14 "Kanto Route 14") to [Fuchsia City](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Fuchsia_City "Fuchsia City").

### Share the Wealth

Enter the gate and speak to another of [Professor Oak](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Professor_Oak "Professor Oak")'s [aides](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Professor%27s_assistant "Professor's assistant"). If you have caught at least 50 different species, the professor has asked him to give you an [Exp. Share](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Exp._Share "Exp. Share"). This item distributes [Experience Points](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Experience "Experience") to all Pokémon in your party whether they battle or not, but reduces the number of points for those that do.

## Fuchsia City

[![](https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/d/d0/Fuchsia_City_FRLG.png/300px-Fuchsia_City_FRLG.png)](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/File:Fuchsia_City_FRLG.png) Fuchsia City

[Fuchsia City](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Fuchsia_City "Fuchsia City") is the largest city in southern [Kanto](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto "Kanto"), located between [Route 18](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto_Route_18 "Kanto Route 18") and [Route 15](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto_Route_15 "Kanto Route 15"). To the south, a beach leads to the waters of [Route 19](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto_Route_19 "Kanto Route 19"). The northern part of the city is occupied by rare Pokémon exhibits and a nature preserve known as the [Safari Zone](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Safari_Zone "Safari Zone"). Trainers aiming to earn their next Badge can challenge the [Fuchsia Gym](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Fuchsia_Gym "Fuchsia Gym") in the southwest.

### Fishing Guru 2

The southeastern-most house belongs to the [Fishing Guru's brother](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Fishing_Brothers "Fishing Brothers"). Speak to him to receive a [Good Rod](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Good_Rod "Good Rod"). This mid-level fishing rod can reel in a greater variety of water-dwelling Pokémon than the [Old Rod](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Old_Rod "Old Rod"). Give it a try at his backyard pond to find [Poliwag](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Poliwag_(Pok%C3%A9mon) "Poliwag (Pokémon)") and [Goldeen](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Goldeen_(Pok%C3%A9mon) "Goldeen (Pokémon)") to add to your collection.

### Safari Zone Warden's house

The southeastern house belongs to [the Safari Zone Warden](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Baoba "Baoba"). It is difficult to understand what he is saying, but seems to have misplaced his set of [Gold Teeth](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Gold_Teeth "Gold Teeth"). If you happen to find a set of false teeth, be sure to return it to him.

### Fuchsia Gym

[![](https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/6/63/Fuchsia_Gym_FRLG.png)](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/File:Fuchsia_Gym_FRLG.png) Fuchsia Gym

**FUCHSIA CITY POKéMON GYM**

**LEADER: KOGA**

The Poisonous Ninja Master!

The [Fuchsia Gym](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Fuchsia_Gym "Fuchsia Gym") officially specializes in [Poison-type](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Poison_(type) "Poison (type)") Pokémon, although there are several [Psychic](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Psychic_(type) "Psychic (type)")\- and [Ground-type](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Ground_(type) "Ground (type)") Pokémon to be found inside. Poison-type moves are super effective against [Grass-type](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Grass_(type) "Grass (type)") Pokémon, while Poison-type Pokémon are weak to Ground- and Psychic-type moves.

The Gym Leader is trained in the skills of the ninja, and has installed a series of nearly invisible glass panels to disorient any challengers. Anyone looking to battle the Gym Leader must first find the path between these panels to reach the middle of the room. [Koga](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Koga "Koga")'s team includes only pure Poison-type Pokémon, but three of his Pokémon have the [Levitate](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Levitate_(Ability) "Levitate (Ability)") Ability, making Psychic-type moves the most effective. Each of his Pokémon can [poison](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Poison_(status_condition) "Poison (status condition)") their target, so be sure to bring along some [Antidotes](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Antidote "Antidote").

After the battle, [Koga](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Koga "Koga") awards you the [Soul Badge](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Badge#Soul_Badge "Badge"), which gives your Pokémon a slight [Defense](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Stat#Defense "Stat") boost during battle and enables the use of [Surf](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Surf_(move) "Surf (move)") in the field. As a prize, he also gives you [TM06](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/TM06 "TM06") ( [Toxic](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Toxic_(move) "Toxic (move)")), which he claims is a secret ninja technique from over 400 years ago.

### Safari Zone

For [$](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_Dollar "Pokémon Dollar") 500, Trainers who visit the [Safari Zone](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Safari_Zone_(Kanto) "Safari Zone (Kanto)") are given 30 [Safari Balls](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Safari_Ball "Safari Ball") and allowed to catch any Pokémon they can find. There is a catch: visitors are restricted from using their own Pokémon to weaken the wild Pokémon first. Instead, they may throw either bait or rocks before attempting capture. Throwing bait makes a Pokémon less likely to run, but harder to catch; throwing a rock has the opposite effect. When visitors run out of Safari Balls or walk 600 steps, the game is over.

| Center Area | Area 1 | Area 2 | Area 3 |

|  | |

#### Center Area

Enter the safari and head to the northeast to reach the second area.

#### Area 1

Climb onto the larger rocky ridge to the south and pick up the [Leaf Stone](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Leaf_Stone "Leaf Stone"). Head west to reach several patches of tall grass, [TM11](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/TM11 "TM11") ( [Sunny Day](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Sunny_Day_(move) "Sunny Day (move)")) on the edge of a lake, and a [Max Potion](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Max_Potion "Max Potion") to the northwest. Collect the [Full Restore](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Full_Restore "Full Restore") near the rest house and take the northwest exit.

#### Area 2

Climb onto the rocky ridge to the east to reach the middle of the zone and a [Quick Claw](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Quick_Claw "Quick Claw"). Backtrack, then go northwest through the tall grass and climb onto the western ridge. Head northeast from the three ponds to find [TM47](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/TM47 "TM47") ( [Steel Wing](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Steel_Wing_(move) "Steel Wing (move)")). Turn west near the rest house to pick up a [Protein](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Protein "Protein") and follow the path to the southwest exit.

#### Area 3

Head south to find a set of [Gold Teeth](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Gold_Teeth "Gold Teeth"), then go west to get [TM32](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/TM32 "TM32") ( [Double Team](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Double_Team_(move) "Double Team (move)")) before entering the Secret House. It seems that no one else has ventured this deep into the park, so the [HM03](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/HM03 "HM03") ( [Surf](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Surf_(move) "Surf (move)")) is yours. Use it on a [Water](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Water_(type) "Water (type)") Pokémon, like [Gyarados](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Gyarados_(Pok%C3%A9mon) "Gyarados (Pokémon)") or [Lapras](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Lapras_(Pok%C3%A9mon) "Lapras (Pokémon)"), and you can cross the pond to the south to reach a [Max Potion](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Max_Potion "Max Potion") and a [Max Revive](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Max_Revive "Max Revive") on the way back to the center. Otherwise, you can backtrack through the other areas until the timer runs out, which likely will not be much longer.

## Route 18

[![](https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/2/2d/Kanto_Route_18_FRLG.png/300px-Kanto_Route_18_FRLG.png)](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/File:Kanto_Route_18_FRLG.png) Route 18

[Route 18](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto_Route_18 "Kanto Route 18") leads west from [Fuchsia City](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Fuchsia_City "Fuchsia City") to [Route 17](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto_Route_17 "Kanto Route 17"). The road northward to [Celadon City](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Celadon_City "Celadon City") can be dangerous for pedestrians, so be sure to bring a [Bicycle](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Bicycle "Bicycle").

| **A colored background means that the Pokémon can be found in this location in the specified game. A white background with a colored letter means that the Pokémon cannot be found here.** | |

### Time for a Trade

Enter the gate and visit the second floor to find a boy who is looking to trade Pokémon. He is hoping to get a [Golduck](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Golduck_(Pok%C3%A9mon) "Golduck (Pokémon)") **[FR](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_FireRed_and_LeafGreen_Versions "Pokémon FireRed and LeafGreen Versions")** / [Slowbro](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Slowbro_(Pok%C3%A9mon) "Slowbro (Pokémon)") **[LG](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Pok%C3%A9mon_FireRed_and_LeafGreen_Versions "Pokémon FireRed and LeafGreen Versions")**, and is willing to trade his [Lickitung](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Lickitung_(Pok%C3%A9mon) "Lickitung (Pokémon)") for one. Both Golduck and Slowbro can be caught in the wild, but Lickitung is a unique Pokémon found nowhere else.

## Route 17

The bridges of [Route 17](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto_Route_17 "Kanto Route 17") pass over the ocean on the way downhill to [Route 18](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto_Route_18 "Kanto Route 18"). Anyone riding a Bicycle on the Cycling Road who stops pedaling will roll southward, unless the A or B Buttons are held.

## Route 16

[![](https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/a/a2/Kanto_Route_16_FRLG.png/300px-Kanto_Route_16_FRLG.png)](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/File:Kanto_Route_16_FRLG.png) Route 16[![](https://archives.bulbagarden.net/media/upload/thumb/1/1a/Kanto_Route_17_FRLG.png/75px-Kanto_Route_17_FRLG.png)](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/File:Kanto_Route_17_FRLG.png) Route 17

[Route 16](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto_Route_16 "Kanto Route 16") leads east from [Route 17](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Kanto_Route_17 "Kanto Route 17") to [Celadon City](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Celadon_City "Celadon City").

### Rags to Riches

Enter the south gate and speak to the Scientist on the upper floor. He happens to be another of [Oak](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Professor_Oak "Professor Oak")'s [aides](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Professor%27s_assistant "Professor's assistant"), and has been instructed to give you an [Amulet Coin](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Amulet_Coin "Amulet Coin") if you have caught at least 40 different Pokémon. When held, the amount of prize money won is doubled if the holder takes part in the battle.

### Roadblock

A [Snorlax](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Snorlax_(Pok%C3%A9mon) "Snorlax (Pokémon)") has fallen asleep near the gate, blocking the path. Use the [Poké Flute](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Pok%C3%A9_Flute "Poké Flute") to wake the Pokémon, which attacks in a grumpy rage! Snorlax are hard to find, so catch it if you can.

### Fly, Fly Away

In the eastern part of the route, use [Cut](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Cut_(move) "Cut (move)") on the small tree to reach the secluded northern area. Enter the house beyond the gate and speak to the girl inside. She prefers to spend time on her own and gives you [HM02](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/HM02 "HM02") ( [Fly](https://bulbapedia.bulbagarden.net/wiki/Fly_(move) "Fly (move)")) to keep her hideaway a secret. Using Fly in the field allows a Trainer to instantly travel to any city or town that had been visited previously.
